      .c__span, [class^=c__span-], [class*=" c__span-"] {␊
        width: calc((99.99999% + var(--col-gap)) * var(--col-span) / var(--col-base) - var(--col-gap));␊
      }␊
      .flow > .c__span, .flow > [class^=c__span-], .flow > [class*=" c__span-"], [class^=flow-] > .c__span, [class^=flow-] > [class^=c__span-], [class^=flow-] > [class*=" c__span-"], [class*=" flow-"] > .c__span, [class*=" flow-"] > [class^=c__span-], [class*=" flow-"] > [class*=" c__span-"] {␊
        width: calc(99.99999% * var(--col-span) / var(--col-base));␊
      }␊
    ␊
      .grid > .c__span, .grid > [class^=c__span-], .grid > [class*=" c__span-"], [class^=grid-] > .c__span, [class^=grid-] > [class^=c__span-], [class^=grid-] > [class*=" c__span-"], [class*=" grid-"] > .c__span, [class*=" grid-"] > [class^=c__span-], [class*=" grid-"] > [class*=" c__span-"] {␊
        width: unset;␊
      }␊
    ␊
      [class^=c__pull-], [class*=" c__pull-"],␊
    [class^=c__push-], [class*=" c__push-"] {␊
        margin-left: calc((99.99999% + var(--col-gap)) * var(--push-l) / var(--col-base));␊
      }␊
      .flow > [class^=c__pull-], .flow > [class*=" c__pull-"], .flow > [class^=c__push-], .flow > [class*=" c__push-"], [class^=flow-] > [class^=c__pull-], [class^=flow-] > [class*=" c__pull-"], [class^=flow-] > [class^=c__push-], [class^=flow-] > [class*=" c__push-"], [class*=" flow-"] > [class^=c__pull-], [class*=" flow-"] > [class*=" c__pull-"], [class*=" flow-"] > [class^=c__push-], [class*=" flow-"] > [class*=" c__push-"] {␊
        margin-left: calc(99.99999% * var(--push-l) / var(--col-base));␊
      }␊
    ␊
      [class^=c__pull-r-], [class*=" c__pull-r-"],␊
    [class^=c__push-r-], [class*=" c__push-r-"] {␊

## output-stack [dartsass]

> Snapshot 1

    `.stack, [class^=stack-], [class*=" stack-"], .plain, [class^=plain-], [class*=" plain-"] {␊
      padding-top: 0.01px;␊
      padding-bottom: 0.01px;␊
    }␊

      margin-bottom: 0;␊
    }␊

      margin-top: var(--stack-gap, var(--inner-y));␊
    }␊
    ␊
    .chain, [class^=chain-], [class*=" chain-"] {␊
      display: flex;␊

    }␊
    .chain > *, [class^=chain-] > *, [class*=" chain-"] > * {␊
      flex: 0 0 auto;␊
      margin-right: 0;␊

    }␊
    .chain > * + *, [class^=chain-] > * + *, [class*=" chain-"] > * + * {␊
      margin-left: var(--chain-gap, var(--inner-x));␊

    ␊
    .stack-0 > * {␊
      --stack-gap: 0;␊

        --outer-left: 200px;␊
        --grid-cols: 12;␊
        --outer-width: 53.3333333333rem;␊
        --breakpoint: 60em;␊
        --inner-y-s: calc(var(--inner-y) * 0.5);␊
        --inner-y-m: 3.5rem;␊
        --inner-y-l: 4px;␊
        --inner-x-s: calc(var(--inner-x) * 0.5);␊
        --inner-x-m: calc(var(--inner-x) * 1);␊
        --inner-x-l: calc(var(--inner-x) * 2);␊
        --outer-width: 53.3333333333rem;␊
      }␊
    }`

## scratch-selectors [dartsass]

> Snapshot 1

    `.stack .f, .stack [class^=f-], .stack [class*=" f-"], [class^=stack-] .f, [class^=stack-] [class^=f-], [class^=stack-] [class*=" f-"], [class*=" stack-"] .f, [class*=" stack-"] [class^=f-], [class*=" stack-"] [class*=" f-"] {␊
      color: blue;␊
    }␊
    ␊
    .a, .b {␊
      color: blue;␊
    }␊
    .c > .e + .a, .c > .e + .b, .d > .e + .a, .d > .e + .b {␊
      color: red;␊
    }␊
    ␊
    .e > .c + .a, .e > .c + .b, .e > .d + .a, .e > .d + .b, .f > .c + .a, .f > .c + .b, .f > .d + .a, .f > .d + .b {␊
      color: red;␊
    }`

## scratch-selectors [libsass]

> Snapshot 1

    `.stack .f, .stack [class^="f-"], .stack [class*=" f-"], [class^="stack-"] .f, [class^="stack-"] [class^="f-"], [class^="stack-"] [class*=" f-"], [class*=" stack-"] .f, [class*=" stack-"] [class^="f-"], [class*=" stack-"] [class*=" f-"] {␊
      color: blue;␊
    }␊
    ␊
    .a, .b {␊
      color: blue;␊
    }␊
    ␊
    .c > .e + .a, .c > .e + .b, .d > .e + .a, .d > .e + .b {␊
      color: red;␊
    }␊
    ␊
    .e > .c + .a, .e > .c + .b, .e > .d + .a, .e > .d + .b, .f > .c + .a, .f > .c + .b, .f > .d + .a, .f > .d + .b {␊
      color: red;␊
    }␊
    `
